  84 <!--
  85 Note: When reading these dates, you should read them as inclusive date ranges.
  86 The date ranges are like date ranges that you see on tomb stones,
  87 but some dates are approximate. Some date ranges overlap due to
  88 revolts, invasions, new constitutions, and slow planned adoption of new currency.
  89 The length of time for these change overs vary widely.
  90 Sometimes, hyperinflation will cause more than one currency to be in effect
  91 in one year. Dates without a "to" attribute mean that the currency is still
  92 in use.
  93 
  94 Dates try to use ISO-8601 style dates, and be accurate as possible.

  86 <!--
  87 Note: When reading these dates, you should read them as inclusive date ranges.
  88 The date ranges are like date ranges that you see on tomb stones,
  89 but some dates are approximate. Some date ranges overlap due to
  90 revolts, invasions, new constitutions, and slow planned adoption of new currency.
  91 The length of time for these change overs vary widely.
  92 Sometimes, hyperinflation will cause more than one currency to be in effect
  93 in one year. Dates without a "to" attribute mean that the currency is still
  94 in use.
  95 
  96 Dates try to use ISO-8601 style dates, and be accurate as possible.
